Caveats:							0	0	
1. Totals and Percent of Total are disabled when data are grouped by a 113 or 130 Cause List because both aggregate and detailed							0	0	
values are displayed in the table. Also be aware that charts and maps containing both aggregate and detail data could be							0	0	
misleading.							0	0	
2. As of April 3, 2017, the underlying cause of death has been revised for 125 deaths in 2014. More information:							0	0	
http://wonder.cdc.gov/wonder/help/ucd.html#2014-Revision.							0	0	
3. Data for Broomfield, Colorado (FIPS code 08014) are only available for 2003 and later; for computational purposes, counts and							0	0	
population estimates for 1999-2002 are set to zero. Thus, counts and rates shown in multi-year requests for this entity do not							0	0	
include any data for years prior to 2003, only data for 2003 and later. More information:							0	0	
http://wonder.cdc.gov/wonder/help/ucd.html#Broomfield.							0	0	
4. There is a discontinuity in the mortality and population data for Adams, Colorado (FIPS code 08001), Boulder, Colorado (FIPS							0	0	
code 08013), Jefferson, Colorado (FIPS code 08059), and Weld, Colorado (FIPS code 080123) between 2002 and 2003. This							0	0	
discontinuity occurs because territory in each of these four counties has been combined to form a new county, Broomfield,							0	0	
Colorado (FIPS code 08014). Beginning in 2003, deaths and population counts for this territory are reported for Broomfield							0	0	
county and are no longer included with data for Adams, Boulder, Jefferson, and Weld.							0	0	
5. Data are Suppressed when the data meet the criteria for confidentiality constraints. More information:							0	0	
http://wonder.cdc.gov/wonder/help/ucd.html#Assurance of Confidentiality.							0	0	
6. Death rates are flagged as Unreliable when the rate is calculated with a numerator of 20 or less. More information:							0	0	
http://wonder.cdc.gov/wonder/help/ucd.html#Unreliable.							0	0
